(***************************************************************************)
(*                                                                         *)
(*   Ancillary file to "An Infinite Family of Elliptic Ladder Integrals"   *)
(*   by Andrew McLeod, Roger Morales, Matt von Hippel, Matthias Wilhelm    *)
(*   and Chi Zhang, arXiv:2301.xxxxx.                                      *)           
(*                                                                         *)
(*   This file contains the result of the 3-loop staggered elliptic        *)
(*   ladder integral I_{L=1,M=1,R=1} as a one-fold integral over           *)
(*   multiple polylogarithms "G", which we denote by "ResultMPL111".       *)
(*   The variables u[i] denote the 7 cross-ratios, and Zeta[i] denotes     *)
(*   the Riemann zeta function.                                            *)
(*   "ellipticP" provides the elliptic curve, and the definition of the    *)
(*   kinematic functions appearing in the argument of the results is given *)
(*   in "cMPLToKinematics111".                                             *)                                             
(*                                                                         *)
(***************************************************************************)


(* This is the elliptic curve y=(x^4+...)^(1/2), given by a quartic polynomial *)

ellipticP=(u[1]^2 - 2*u[1]^2*u[2] + u[1]^2*u[2]^2 + 2*u[1]*v[2] + 2*x*u[1]*v[2] + 
  2*x*u[1]^2*v[2] - 2*u[1]*u[2]*v[2] - 4*x*u[1]*u[2]*v[2] - 
  2*x*u[1]^2*u[2]*v[2] + 2*x*u[1]*u[2]^2*v[2] - 2*u[1]*u[3]*v[2] + 
  2*u[1]*u[2]*u[3]*v[2] + 4*u[1]*u[2]*u[4]*v[2] + 2*x*u[1]*u[2]*u[4]*v[2] - 
  2*x*u[1]*u[2]^2*u[4]*v[2] - 2*u[1]*v[1]*v[2] - 2*x*u[1]*v[1]*v[2] - 
  2*u[1]*u[2]*v[1]*v[2] + 2*x*u[1]*u[2]*v[1]*v[2] + v[2]^2 + 2*x*v[2]^2 + 
  x^2*v[2]^2 + 4*x*u[1]*v[2]^2 + 4*x^2*u[1]*v[2]^2 + x^2*u[1]^2*v[2]^2 - 
  2*x*u[2]*v[2]^2 - 2*x^2*u[2]*v[2]^2 - 2*x*u[1]*u[2]*v[2]^2 - 
  4*x^2*u[1]*u[2]*v[2]^2 + x^2*u[2]^2*v[2]^2 - 2*u[3]*v[2]^2 - 
  2*x*u[3]*v[2]^2 - 4*x*u[1]*u[3]*v[2]^2 + 2*x*u[2]*u[3]*v[2]^2 + 
  2*x*u[1]*u[2]*u[3]*v[2]^2 + u[3]^2*v[2]^2 + 2*x*u[2]*u[4]*v[2]^2 + 
  2*x^2*u[2]*u[4]*v[2]^2 + 4*x*u[1]*u[2]*u[4]*v[2]^2 + 
  2*x^2*u[1]*u[2]*u[4]*v[2]^2 - 2*x^2*u[2]^2*u[4]*v[2]^2 + 
  2*x*u[2]*u[3]*u[4]*v[2]^2 + x^2*u[2]^2*u[4]^2*v[2]^2 - 2*v[1]*v[2]^2 - 
  4*x*v[1]*v[2]^2 - 2*x^2*v[1]*v[2]^2 - 2*x*u[1]*v[1]*v[2]^2 - 
  2*x^2*u[1]*v[1]*v[2]^2 + 2*x*u[2]*v[1]*v[2]^2 + 2*x^2*u[2]*v[1]*v[2]^2 + 
  2*u[3]*v[1]*v[2]^2 + 2*x*u[3]*v[1]*v[2]^2 - 4*x*u[2]*u[3]*v[1]*v[2]^2 - 
  2*x*u[2]*u[4]*v[1]*v[2]^2 - 2*x^2*u[2]*u[4]*v[1]*v[2]^2 + v[1]^2*v[2]^2 + 
  2*x*v[1]^2*v[2]^2 + x^2*v[1]^2*v[2]^2 + 2*x*v[2]^3 + 4*x^2*v[2]^3 + 
  2*x^3*v[2]^3 + 2*x^2*u[1]*v[2]^3 + 2*x^3*u[1]*v[2]^3 - 2*x^2*u[2]*v[2]^3 - 
  2*x^3*u[2]*v[2]^3 - 4*x*u[3]*v[2]^3 - 4*x^2*u[3]*v[2]^3 - 
  2*x^2*u[1]*u[3]*v[2]^3 + 2*x^2*u[2]*u[3]*v[2]^3 + 2*x*u[3]^2*v[2]^3 + 
  2*x^2*u[2]*u[4]*v[2]^3 + 2*x^3*u[2]*u[4]*v[2]^3 + 
  2*x^2*u[2]*u[3]*u[4]*v[2]^3 - 2*x*v[1]*v[2]^3 - 4*x^2*v[1]*v[2]^3 - 
  2*x^3*v[1]*v[2]^3 + 2*x*u[3]*v[1]*v[2]^3 + 2*x^2*u[3]*v[1]*v[2]^3 + 
  x^2*v[2]^4 + 2*x^3*v[2]^4 + x^4*v[2]^4 - 2*x^2*u[3]*v[2]^4 - 
  2*x^3*u[3]*v[2]^4 + x^2*u[3]^2*v[2]^4)^(1/2)/v[2]^2


(* This is the map from the coefficients to the kinematics *)

cMPLToKinematics111={{cMPL[1], 0}, {cMPL[2], 1}, {cMPL[3], x/(1 + x)}, 
 {cMPL[4], (-1 + u[3])/u[3]}, {cMPL[5], u[3]}, {cMPL[6], u[4]/(-1 + u[4])}, 
 {cMPL[7], -((u[4]*(-1 + u[5]))/(-1 + u[4]))}, 
 {cMPL[8], x/((1 + x)*u[4]*u[5])}, 
 {cMPL[9], (u[4]*(-1 + u[3]*u[5]))/(1 - u[4] + u[3]*u[4]*u[5])}, 
 {cMPL[10], (u[4]*(x + u[3]*u[5]))/(-x + x*u[4] + u[3]*u[4]*u[5])}, 
 {cMPL[11], u[1]/(x*v[2])}, {cMPL[12], u[1]/(u[3]*u[4]*u[5]*v[2])}, 
 {cMPL[13], (1 + x*v[2])/u[2]}, {cMPL[14], (1 + x*v[2])/(u[2]*u[4]*u[5])}, 
 {cMPL[15], (u[1] + x*v[2])/u[1]}, 
 {cMPL[16], (u[2]*u[4]*u[5] - v[1])/(1 - v[1] + x*v[2])}, 
 {cMPL[17], -(v[1]/(1 - v[1] + x*v[2]))}, 
 {cMPL[18], (u[2]*u[4] - v[1])/(1 - u[2] + u[2]*u[4] - v[1] + x*v[2])}, 
 {cMPL[19], (u[2]*u[3]*u[4]*u[5] - v[1])/(1 + u[2]*u[3]*u[4]*u[5] - v[1] + 
    x*v[2])}, {cMPL[20], (x*u[2]*u[4] + u[2]*u[3]*u[4]*u[5] - v[1] - x*v[1])/
   (1 + x - x*u[2] + x*u[2]*u[4] + u[2]*u[3]*u[4]*u[5] - v[1] - x*v[1] + 
    x*v[2] + x^2*v[2])}, {cMPL[21], (u[1] + v[2] + x*v[2] - u[3]*v[2])/
   (u[1] - u[3]*v[2])}, {cMPL[22], (-u[1] - x*u[3]*v[2])/
   (x*(u[1] - u[3]*v[2]))}, {cMPL[23], u[1]/(u[1] + x*u[3]*v[2])}, 
 {cMPL[24], ((1 + x)*u[1])/(u[1] + x*u[3]*v[2])}, 
 {cMPL[25], (u[1] + x*u[3]*v[2])/(x*u[3]*v[2])}, 
 {cMPL[26], (u[4]*(u[1] - u[3]*u[5]*v[2]))/(u[1]*(-1 + u[4]))}, 
 {cMPL[27], -((u[4]*(-u[1] + u[1]*u[3]*u[5] - x*u[3]*v[2] + 
      x*u[3]*u[5]*v[2]))/(-u[1] + u[1]*u[4] - u[1]*u[3]*u[4]*u[5] - 
     x*u[3]*v[2] + x*u[3]*u[4]*v[2]))}, 
 {cMPL[28], -((u[3]*u[4]*u[5]*v[2])/(u[1] - u[3]*u[4]*u[5]*v[2]))}, 
 {cMPL[29], -(u[1]/(-u[1] - x*u[3]*v[2] + x*u[3]*u[4]*u[5]*v[2]))}, 
 {cMPL[30], (-u[1] - x*u[3]*v[2] + x*u[3]*u[4]*u[5]*v[2])/
   (x*u[3]*(-1 + u[4]*u[5])*v[2])}, 
 {cMPL[31], -((u[4]*(-u[1] + u[1]*u[3]*u[5] - x*u[3]*v[2] + u[3]*u[5]*v[2] + 
      x*u[3]*u[5]*v[2] - u[3]^2*u[5]*v[2]))/(-u[1] + u[1]*u[4] - 
     u[1]*u[3]*u[4]*u[5] - x*u[3]*v[2] + x*u[3]*u[4]*v[2] + 
     u[3]^2*u[4]*u[5]*v[2]))}, 
 {cMPL[32], (u[1]*u[2]*u[4] - u[1]*v[1] - u[2]*u[3]*u[4]*u[5]*v[2] + 
    u[3]*v[1]*v[2])/(u[1] - u[1]*u[2] + u[1]*u[2]*u[4] - u[1]*v[1] + 
    x*u[1]*v[2] - u[3]*v[2] + u[3]*v[1]*v[2] - x*u[3]*v[2]^2)}, 
 {cMPL[33], (2*(u[1]*u[2]*u[4] - u[1]*v[1] + x*u[2]*u[4]*v[2] - v[1]*v[2] - 
     x*v[1]*v[2] + u[3]*v[1]*v[2]))/(u[1] - u[1]*u[2] + 2*u[1]*u[2]*u[4] - 
    2*u[1]*v[1] + v[2] + x*v[2] + x*u[1]*v[2] - x*u[2]*v[2] - u[3]*v[2] + 
    x*u[2]*u[4]*v[2] - v[1]*v[2] - x*v[1]*v[2] + 2*u[3]*v[1]*v[2] + 
    ellipticP*v[2]^2 + x*v[2]^2 + x^2*v[2]^2 - x*u[3]*v[2]^2)}, 
 {cMPL[34], (-2*(u[1]*u[2]*u[4] - u[1]*v[1] + x*u[2]*u[4]*v[2] - v[1]*v[2] - 
     x*v[1]*v[2] + u[3]*v[1]*v[2]))/(-u[1] + u[1]*u[2] - 2*u[1]*u[2]*u[4] + 
    2*u[1]*v[1] - v[2] - x*v[2] - x*u[1]*v[2] + x*u[2]*v[2] + u[3]*v[2] - 
    x*u[2]*u[4]*v[2] + v[1]*v[2] + x*v[1]*v[2] - 2*u[3]*v[1]*v[2] + 
    ellipticP*v[2]^2 - x*v[2]^2 - x^2*v[2]^2 + x*u[3]*v[2]^2)}, 
 {cMPL[35], (-u[1] + u[1]*u[2] - x*u[1]*v[2] - x*u[3]*v[2] + 
    x*u[2]*u[3]*v[2] - u[2]*u[3]*u[4]*u[5]*v[2] - x^2*u[3]*v[2]^2)/
   (u[1]*u[2]*u[4] - u[1]*v[1] + x*u[2]*u[3]*u[4]*v[2] - 
    u[2]*u[3]*u[4]*u[5]*v[2] + u[2]*u[3]^2*u[4]*u[5]*v[2] - 
    x*u[3]*v[1]*v[2])}, {cMPL[36], (-u[1] - x*u[1]*v[2] - x*u[3]*v[2] + 
    x*u[2]*u[3]*u[4]*u[5]*v[2] - x^2*u[3]*v[2]^2)/
   (x*(u[1] - u[1]*u[2] + x*u[1]*v[2] - u[3]*v[2] + 
     u[2]*u[3]*u[4]*u[5]*v[2] - x*u[3]*v[2]^2))}, 
 {cMPL[37], (u[1]*(1 + x*v[2]))/(u[1] + x*u[1]*v[2] + x*u[3]*v[2] - 
    x*u[2]*u[3]*u[4]*u[5]*v[2] + x^2*u[3]*v[2]^2)}, 
 {cMPL[38], (u[1]*(1 + x - x*u[2] + x*v[2] + x^2*v[2]))/
   (u[1] + x*u[1]*v[2] + x*u[3]*v[2] - x*u[2]*u[3]*u[4]*u[5]*v[2] + 
    x^2*u[3]*v[2]^2)}, {cMPL[39], (u[1] + x*u[1]*v[2] + x*u[3]*v[2] - 
    x*u[2]*u[3]*u[4]*u[5]*v[2] + x^2*u[3]*v[2]^2)/
   (x*u[3]*v[2]*(1 - u[2]*u[4]*u[5] + x*v[2]))}, 
 {cMPL[40], (u[1]*u[2]*u[3]*u[4]*u[5] - u[1]*v[1] + 
    x*u[2]*u[3]*u[4]*u[5]*v[2] - x*u[3]*v[1]*v[2])/
   (u[1] + u[1]*u[2]*u[3]*u[4]*u[5] - u[1]*v[1] + x*u[1]*v[2] + x*u[3]*v[2] - 
    x*u[3]*v[1]*v[2] + x^2*u[3]*v[2]^2)}, 
 {cMPL[41], (u[1]*u[2]*u[4] - u[1]*v[1] + x*u[2]*u[3]*u[4]*v[2] - 
    u[2]*u[3]*u[4]*u[5]*v[2] + u[2]*u[3]^2*u[4]*u[5]*v[2] - x*u[3]*v[1]*v[2])/
   (u[1] - u[1]*u[2] + u[1]*u[2]*u[4] - u[1]*v[1] + x*u[1]*v[2] + 
    x*u[3]*v[2] - x*u[2]*u[3]*v[2] + x*u[2]*u[3]*u[4]*v[2] + 
    u[2]*u[3]^2*u[4]*u[5]*v[2] - x*u[3]*v[1]*v[2] + x^2*u[3]*v[2]^2)}}


(* This is the 3-loop result as a one-fold integral over MPLs *)

ResultMPL111=(3*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[1], cMPL[22]}, 1] + 
 3*G[{cMPL[31], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[1], cMPL[22]}, 1] - 
 3*G[{cMPL[33], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[1], cMPL[22]}, 1] - 
 3*G[{cMPL[34], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[1], cMPL[22]}, 1] - 
 2*G[{cMPL[18], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[1], cMPL[30]}, 1] - 
 2*G[{cMPL[31], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[1], cMPL[30]}, 1] + 
 2*G[{cMPL[33], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[1], cMPL[30]}, 1] + 
 2*G[{cMPL[34], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[1], cMPL[30]}, 1] + 
 2*G[{cMPL[18], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[1], cMPL[39]}, 1] - 
 2*G[{cMPL[33], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[1], cMPL[39]}, 1] - 
 2*G[{cMPL[34], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[1], cMPL[39]}, 1] + 
 2*G[{cMPL[40], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[1], cMPL[39]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[2], cMPL[25]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[2], cMPL[25]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[2], cMPL[36]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[32], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[2], cMPL[36]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[33], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[2], cMPL[36]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[34], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[2], cMPL[36]}, 1] + 
 3*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[22], cMPL[2]}, 1] + 
 3*G[{cMPL[31], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[22], cMPL[2]}, 1] - 
 3*G[{cMPL[33], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[22], cMPL[2]}, 1] - 
 3*G[{cMPL[34], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[22], cMPL[2]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[22], cMPL[22]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[31], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[22], cMPL[22]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[33], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[22], cMPL[22]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[34], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[22], cMPL[22]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[25], cMPL[2]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[25], cMPL[2]}, 1] - 
 2*G[{cMPL[18], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[30], cMPL[2]}, 1] - 
 2*G[{cMPL[31], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[30], cMPL[2]}, 1] + 
 2*G[{cMPL[33], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[30], cMPL[2]}, 1] + 
 2*G[{cMPL[34], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[30], cMPL[2]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[36], cMPL[2]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[32], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[36], cMPL[2]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[33], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[36], cMPL[2]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[34], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[36], cMPL[2]}, 1] + 
 2*G[{cMPL[18], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[39], cMPL[2]}, 1] - 
 2*G[{cMPL[33], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[39], cMPL[2]}, 1] - 
 2*G[{cMPL[34], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[39], cMPL[2]}, 1] + 
 2*G[{cMPL[40], cMPL[41]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[39], cMPL[2]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[22]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[4], cMPL[41]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[28]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[4], cMPL[41]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[30]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[4], cMPL[41]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[39]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[4], cMPL[41]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[22], cMPL[30]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[4], cMPL[41]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[25], cMPL[30]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[4], cMPL[41]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[25], cMPL[39]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[4], cMPL[41]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[28], cMPL[30]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[4], cMPL[41]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[22]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[18], cMPL[41]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[28]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[18], cMPL[41]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[30]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[18], cMPL[41]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[39]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[18], cMPL[41]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[22], cMPL[30]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[18], cMPL[41]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[25], cMPL[30]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[18], cMPL[41]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[25], cMPL[39]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[18], cMPL[41]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[28], cMPL[30]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[18], cMPL[41]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[22]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[31], cMPL[41]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[28]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[31], cMPL[41]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[30]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[31], cMPL[41]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[22], cMPL[30]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[31], cMPL[41]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[25], cMPL[30]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[31], cMPL[41]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[28], cMPL[30]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[31], cMPL[41]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[22]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[33], cMPL[41]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[28]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[33], cMPL[41]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[30]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[33], cMPL[41]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[39]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[33], cMPL[41]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[22], cMPL[30]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[33], cMPL[41]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[25], cMPL[30]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[33], cMPL[41]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[25], cMPL[39]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[33], cMPL[41]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[28], cMPL[30]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[33], cMPL[41]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[22]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[34], cMPL[41]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[28]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[34], cMPL[41]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[30]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[34], cMPL[41]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[1], cMPL[39]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[34], cMPL[41]}, 1] - 
 G[{cMPL[22], cMPL[30]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[34], cMPL[41]}, 1] + 
 G[{cMPL[25], cMPL[30]}, 1]*G[{cMPL[4], cMPL[34], cMPL[41]}, 1] -
